e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX; } function getClientY(e) { return e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientY : e.clientY; } function onMove(e) { if (!isDragging) return; // prevent default touch behavior while dragging if (e.cancelable) e.preventDefault(); const visibleEdge = 40; const minX = -el.offsetWidth + visibleEdge; const maxX = window.innerWidth - visibleEdge; const minY = -el.offsetHeight + visibleEdge; const maxY = window.innerHeight - visibleEdge; el.style.left = `${Math.max(minX, Math.min(getClientX(e) - offsetX, maxX))}px`; el.style.top = `${Math.max(minY, Math.min(getClientY(e) - offsetY, maxY))}px`; el.style.bottom = "auto"; el.style.right = "auto"; } function onUp() { isDragging = false; document.removeEventListener("mousemove", onMove); document.removeEventListener("mouseup", onUp); document.removeEventListener("touchmove", onMove); document.removeEventListener("touchend", onUp); } function onDown(e) { // don't drag if clicking buttons, links, or inside the dropdown if (e.target.closest('button') || e.target.closest('a') || e.target.closest('.dropdown-menu')) return; isDragging = true; const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect(); offsetX = getClientX(e) - rect.left; offsetY = getClientY(e) - rect.top; document.addEventListener("mousemove", onMove, { passive: false }); document.addEventListener("mouseup", onUp); document.addEventListener("touchmove", onMove, { passive: false }); document.addEventListener("touchend", onUp); } el.addEventListener("mousedown", onDown); el.addEventListener("touchstart", onDown, { passive: false }); } function toggleGameStatsPopup() { const popup = document.getElementById("gameStatsPopup"); if (!popup) return; const showing = popup.style.display === "none"; popup.style.display = showing ? "flex" : "none"; if (showing) updateGameStatsPopup(); } function injectGameStatsButton() { if (document.getElementById("btn_game_stats")) return; const anchor = document.getElementById("view_electoral_map"); } } }); } campaignTrail_temp.cyoa = true; // pk -> index lookup for questions let _questionIdxByPk = null; function _rebuildQuestionIdxMap() { _questionIdxByPk = new Map(); const arr = campaignTrail_temp.questions_json; for (let i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) { _questionIdxByPk.set(Number(arr[i].pk), i); } } // returns the true array index (>= 0) or -1 if not found function getQuestionIndexFromPk(pk) { const n = Number(pk); })(); // Tooltip code function escapeRegex(str) { return str.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&'); } function getTooltips(str) { const matches = []; tooltipList.forEach((tooltip, index) => { const safeSearch = escapeRegex(tooltip.searchString); const regex = new RegExp( `(?<=\\b|\\s|^|“)${safeSearch}(?=[.,;!?]?\\b|\\s|”|$)`, 'g' ); let match; while ((match = regex.exec(str)) !== null) { matches.push({ start: match.index, end: match.index + match[0].length, tooltipIndex: index }); } }); matches.sort((a, b) => { if (a.start !== b.start) return a.start - b.start; return (b.end - b.start) - (a.end - a.start); }); for (let i = 0; i < matches.length - 1;) { if (matches[i + 1].start < matches[i].end) { matches.splice(i + 1, 1); } else { i++; } } return matches; } function applyTooltips(str) { const matches = getTooltips(str); let result = ''; let lastIndex = 0; matches.forEach(match => { const tooltip = tooltipList[match.tooltipIndex]; const safeExplanation = tooltip.explanationText .replace(//gi, "") .replace(/<\/div>/gi, ""); result += str.slice(lastIndex, match.start); result += `${tooltip.searchString}${safeExplanation}`; lastIndex = match.end; }); result += str.slice(lastIndex); return result; } function applyTooltipsToObject(obj) { for (const key of Object.keys(obj)) { if (typeof obj[key] === 'string') { obj[key] = applyTooltips(obj[key]); } else if (obj[key] && typeof obj[key] === 'object') { applyTooltipsToObject(obj[key]); } } } applyTooltipsToObject(campaignTrail_temp.questions_json); applyTooltipsToObject(campaignTrail_temp.answers_json); applyTooltipsToObject(campaignTrail_temp.answer_feedback_json); // This is a dynamic election night thingy, // similar to that of The Political Process // taken from 2012LBM (function () { if (!window.campaignTrail_temp?.dynamicEN) return; } const sortedCands = getSortedCands(); const activeStates = isGeneral ? campaignTrail_temp.states_json : states; const someStatesHaveEVs = activeStates.some((f) => f.fields.electoral_votes > 0); const stateMap = mapPkToFields(activeStates); // reset simulation vars activeStateAbbr = null; isPaused = false; tickRate = 1000; currentTickState = {}; stateBiases = {}; stateNextUpdate = {}; // mirages! // for every state, we decide *how* it reports (e.g. urban dump, rural mirage, steady) activeStates.forEach(s => { const resData = campaignTrail_temp.final_state_results.find(r => r.state === s.pk); if (!resData) return; // find actual winner and runner up let sortedRes = [...resData.result].sort((a, b) => b.votes - a.votes); let winner = sortedRes[0].candidate; let runnerUp = sortedRes.length > 1 ? sortedRes[1].candidate : winner; // randomly pick a scenario let rand = Math.random(); let biasCand = winner; let strength = 0; if (rand < 0.35) { // mirage (loser leads early) biasCand = runnerUp; strength = 0.15 + (Math.random() * 0.25); } else if (rand < 0.65) { // dominance (winner leads even more early) biasCand = winner; strength = 0.10 + (Math.random() * 0.15); } else { // balanced (roughly accurate from start) strength = 0.02; } stateBiases[s.pk] = { biasCandidate: biasCand, biasStrength: strength, // random reporting curve speed (0.8 = fast start, 1.2 = slow start) reportingSpeed: 0.8 + (Math.random() * 0.4) }; }); const s = PROPS.ELECTIONS.get(String(campaignTrail_temp.election_id)); const winningEV = s.winning_electoral_vote_number; const evsToWin = `${someStatesHaveEVs ? `

$("#map_footer").html("Processing results..."); if (isGeneral) { handleFinalResults(10000); m(); } else { campaignTrail_temp.question_number++; nextQuestion(); } }); // calc snapshot for a state function calculateStateSnapshot(resData, currTime, closeTime, callTime, prevSnapshot) { if (currTime < closeTime) { return { pk: resData.state, isReporting: false, isCalled: false, pctReporting: 0, votes: resData.result.map(r => ({ ...r, sim_votes: 0 })), leader: null }; } const isCalled = (currTime >= callTime); // reporting % // we use a curve so it starts slow and speeds up (or vice versa based on random speed) let rawProgress = (currTime - closeTime) / (callTime - closeTime); if (isCalled) rawProgress = 1.0; const biasData = stateBiases[resData.state]; // reporting speed variance let adjustedProgress = Math.pow(rawProgress, biasData.reportingSpeed); if (adjustedProgress > 1) adjustedProgress = 1; if (adjustedProgress < 0) adjustedProgress = 0; // total votes counted so far const totalCounted = Math.floor(resData.total_votes_final * adjustedProgress); // vote shares with bias // if progress is low, bias strength is high. as progress -> 1, bias -> 0 let decay = Math.pow(1 - adjustedProgress, 2); // bias falls off quadratically let simResults = resData.result.map(r => { // get actual final percentage let finalShare = r.votes / resData.total_votes_final; if (isNaN(finalShare)) finalShare = 0; let currentShare = finalShare; if (!isCalled) { // apply mirage if (r.candidate === biasData.biasCandidate) { currentShare += (biasData.biasStrength * decay); } // random noise (high noise early, low noise late) let noise = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.05 * decay; currentShare += noise; if (currentShare < 0) currentShare = 0; } else { currentShare = finalShare; // exact match when called } return { candidate: r.candidate, share: currentShare, final_votes: r.votes }; }); // normalize shares let totalShare = simResults.reduce((a, b) => a + b.share, 0); if (totalShare === 0) totalShare = 1; let finalSimulatedVotes = simResults.map(r => { let normalizedShare = r.share / totalShare; let votes = Math.floor(totalCounted * normalizedShare); // cap at final votes so a small candidate can't exceed their total if (votes > r.final_votes) { votes = r.final_votes; } // ensure votes don't go down from previous tick if (prevSnapshot) { let prevData = prevSnapshot.votes.find(p => p.candidate === r.candidate); if (prevData && votes < prevData.sim_votes) { votes = prevData.sim_votes; } } return { candidate: r.candidate, sim_votes: votes, percent: (normalizedShare * 100) }; }); // find leader let leader = null; let maxV = -1; finalSimulatedVotes.forEach(r => { if (r.sim_votes > maxV) { maxV = r.sim_votes; leader = r.candidate; } }); return { pk: resData.state, isReporting: true, isCalled: isCalled, pctReporting: Math.floor(adjustedProgress * 100), votes: finalSimulatedVotes, leader: leader, final_winner: resData.final_winner };     “Several high-ranking members of Congress have been suspected of involvement in a sex trafficking ring and have been accordingly investigated,” according to a statement released by the Director of the FBI.

    The arrests included the former Presidential candidate, Senator Josh Hawley of Missouri, Senator Mike Lee of Utah, and Chairman of the Republican National Committee Elise Stefanik.

    According to further statements by the Assistant Director and other Federal officials, the arrests are expected to expand to additionally include Democratic Party suspects as well as others. The most notable amongst these being former Presidential Nominee Hillary Clinton, who was caught fleeing the country from the JFK International Airport last week at 8:13 PM, US Eastern Standard Time.

    According to CNN, the interim Republican National Committee has issued a condemnation of the arrests as part of an organized effort against political opponents of the Ocasio-Cortez administration.

    This incident, occurring during the preparations for the 2038 midterms, will surely send a shockwave through American politics. Political analysts from the American MSNBC news agency have noted the increasingly politicized usage of the American security services, claiming that such usage would damage the integrity of the American democratic system.

    President Ocasio-Cortez has not personally commented on the situation, with her weekly Tiktok chats scheduled for the 29th at the earliest. Vice President Jon Ossoff has been quoted as saying that "the obstructionism of the Republican Party cannot be tolerated during this current state of emergency, with tensions rising in our allies, and with our enemies."

    This statement seems to suggest frustration regarding the failure of last week’s vote on the Filipino Crisis, as the new government has continued its blockade of American installations in the archipelago. Pressure by American lobbyist groups has grown to support greater involvement in the area, something which the Republican Party have pushed heavily to resist in the past.
